	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<form role="search" method="get" action="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/" class="wp-block-search__button-outside wp-block-search__text-button alignright wp-block-search"    ><label class="wp-block-search__label screen-reader-text" for="wp-block-search__input-1" >Search</label><div class="wp-block-search__inside-wrapper"  style="width: 329px"><input class="wp-block-search__input" id="wp-block-search__input-1" placeholder="" value="" type="search" name="s" required /><button aria-label="Search" class="wp-block-search__button wp-element-button" type="submit" >Search</button></div></form>

<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" width="600" height="315" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20600%20315'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Sherry and Shelby (a black yorkiepoo) on a beach with &quot;Digital Nomad and a Dog&quot; written in a pretty script." class="wp-image-67939" data-lazy-srcset="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px.webp 600w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px-300x158.webp 300w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" data-lazy-src="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="600" height="315" src="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px.webp" alt="Sherry and Shelby (a black yorkiepoo) on a beach with &quot;Digital Nomad and a Dog&quot; written in a pretty script." class="wp-image-67939" srcset="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px.webp 600w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/07/Cover-Photo-600-×-315-px-300x158.webp 300w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<p>I&#8217;m Sherry and that cute fluff ball is Shelby. I became a digital nomad at the age of 53 and have been slowly traveling through Mexico ever since (going on three years now!). I&#8217;m here to help you live your dream of traveling the world, with or without a dog.</p>



<p>Whether you want to be a digital nomad and travel full-time or just want some epic vacations, I&#8217;ve got you covered! <a href="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/about-me/">Learn more about me here.</a></p>

<div class="wp-block-media-text alignwide has-media-on-the-right is-stacked-on-mobile" style="grid-template-columns:auto 27%"><div class="wp-block-media-text__content">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">You can live this life too!</h2>



<p><strong><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Youll-Murdered-Drug-Cartel-other-ebook/dp/B0BSXSWD2P/ref=cm_cr_arp_d_product_top?ie=UTF8" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Get your copy of my book at Amazon.com</a>.</strong></p>



<p>Are you working at a soul-sucking job counting down to retirement? Dreaming about the day you can finally travel to those wonderful places you see in movies?</p>



<p>Guess what… you don’t have to wait.</p>



<p>You can travel full-time while working NOW. I know it’s possible because I’m doing it!</p>



<p>This book will walk you through every step you need to take:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Get a job</li>



<li>Get insurance</li>



<li>Where to go</li>



<li>How to survive when you get there</li>



<li>And what about all your stuff???</li>
</ul>
</div><figure class="wp-block-media-text__media"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Youll-Murdered-Drug-Cartel-other-ebook/dp/B0BSXSWD2P/ref=tmm_kin_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&amp;qid=1674655029&amp;sr=8-1" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><img decoding="async" width="642" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20642%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Book cover" class="wp-image-993 size-large" data-lazy-srcset="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-642x1024.webp 642w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-188x300.webp 188w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-768x1226.webp 768w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-963x1536.webp 963w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-1283x2048.webp 1283w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover.webp 1410w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px" data-lazy-src="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-642x1024.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="642" height="1024" src="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-642x1024.webp" alt="Book cover" class="wp-image-993 size-large" srcset="https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-642x1024.webp 642w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-188x300.webp 188w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-768x1226.webp 768w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-963x1536.webp 963w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover-1283x2048.webp 1283w,https://digitalnomadandadog.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/Book-cover.webp 1410w" sizes="(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px" /></noscript></a></figure></div>
